## bloody mach
4) Anibal b Negro Navarro [UWA JLH]
## Anibal came in as champion. Negro took the first, Anibal took the second and dominated the third. He was about to win when Texano (Navarro's second) distracted the ref to set up an illegal Navarro punch, which gave him the win and the title. Negro's first singles title, the only Misionero not to have captured one yet.
5) Villano I, Villano III, Villano IV DQ Canek, Fishman, Tamba
## Fishman pulled Villano III's masks

## La Fiera was scheduled, ruled medically unable to compete by Dr. Horacio Ramirez of the commission. Fiera came to the ring anyway, with EMLL's Juan Herrera coming out to escort Fiera to the back and replace him with Supremo. Fans revolted, and Fiera was allowed to wrestle to prevent a serious situation. Box y Lucha brings up a recent (May) disaster at a Mexico football stadium as a reason EMLL might have wanted to appease the crowd. They're also very high on Kiss.
